  <script>



	function sleep(ms) {

		return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms))

	}



	const changeFontSize = () => {

		const componentSplitPayment = document.getElementsByTagName('split-payment-cta')[0].shadowRoot.children[0]

		const splitPaymentFontSize = (fontSize) => {

			componentSplitPayment.style.fontSize = fontSize

			componentSplitPayment.getElementsByTagName('button')[0].style.fontSize = fontSize

		}

		splitPaymentFontSize('12px')

	}



	async function doFunctionWithRetries(callback, interval) {

		let attempts = 5

		let timeToLoad = 0

		let succeed = false

		while (attempts > 0 && !succeed) {

			try {

				callback()

				succeed = true

			} catch (e) {

				timeToLoad += interval

				await sleep(timeToLoad)

				attempts -= 1

			}

		}

	}



	const removeFullscreenModal = () => {

		document.getElementsByTagName('split-payment-cta')[0].shadowRoot.children[0].getElementsByClassName('cta__opener')[0].addEventListener('click', () => {

			const removeFullScreen = () => document.getElementsByTagName('split-payment-cta')[0].shadowRoot.children[1].shadowRoot.children[0].getElementsByClassName('modal')[0].classList.remove('fullscreen-modal')

			doFunctionWithRetries(removeFullScreen, 1000)

		})

	}



	doFunctionWithRetries(changeFontSize, 1000)

	doFunctionWithRetries(removeFullscreenModal, 1000)
